ç‚¹æˆ‘è·³è½¬steamGlobal Positions(å…¨çƒèŒä½)
åŸæ–‡ï¼š

Map sharing works again! You donâ€™t even need to be in the
A New Reign beta
anymore!
Code contributions are welcome:
https://github.com/rezecib/GlobalPositions
Features
Show other players on the map (and hover over them to see who they are).
Show player indicators (the bubble things on the side of the screen) when theyâ€™re far away.
Light signal fires that show up as indicators and on the map.
Ping the map by alt+clicking, creating markers that show other players points of interest. Note that muting a player hides their pings. Controller users can ping by clicking in the right stick.
Optout of sharing your location with a button on the scoreboard.
Share your map discovery with other players automatically
Wilderness Mode
By default, if you play in Wilderness Mode, it will ignore most of the config options. If you want to override that, set the Wilderness Mode Override to Enabled. Otherwise, it will hide player positions, but always show campfires.
Configuration Options
On the mods screen, with this mod selected, you can change a lot of the settings with the â€œConfigureâ€ button.
Player Indicators
Always
makes it so player indicators always show.
Scoreboard
(default) only shows them when you bring up the scoreboard.
Disabled
removes both the indicators and the map icons.
Player Icons
Show
(default) will show playerâ€™s map icons on the map.
Hide
will hide them.
Show Fires
Always
means they always produce smoke signals when theyâ€™re lit, so show up globally regardless of fuel used.
Charcoal
(default) means you have to fuel them with charcoal to produce smoke signals.
Disabled
turns off smoke signals entirely.
Fire Icons
Show
(default) shows fire icons on the map when they are smoking.
Hide
doesnâ€™t show them even if theyâ€™re smoking
Share Map
Enabled
(default) makes it so that as other players explore the world, your map will update too. Note that this will only work if players or icons are set to be shown.
Wilderness Override
Disabled
(default) makes it so that in Wilderness Mode,
Show Fires
is set to
Always
, and
Player Icons
and
Player Indicators
are
Disabled
. This adds some risk of discovery to making fires, so cook with caution!
Enabled
makes it use whatever settings you have set yourself, rather than that Wilderness preset.
Pings
Enabled
(default) allows players to alt+click the map to ping areas for others to see.
Disabled
doesnâ€™t allow pings at all.
Most options are only used by the host; if youâ€™re joining, the only option that gets read is whether to show the player indicators at all times or only on the scoreboard.
A huge thanks to Sarcen for figuring out his very clever system for getting player icons to show on the map globally for clients!

Please make Jesus Lord of your life today, I love you!
Note: If some of the slots are off screen or hidden by the crafting menu,go ingame main screen to options\settings\hud and lower the hud size.
The Storm Cellar is fireproof.
The Storm Cellar is a massive storage hole with 80 slots
The Storm Cellar has fridge function with option to disable if ya want.
The Storm Cellar is craftable under the Structures Tab
Recipe = 20 cut stone,20 wood flooring and 1 gold shovel
There are 2 condfigurations for the slots
Default 5x16
8x10 for low resolution monitors.
Added workable option in mod config. If Nope is chosen in the config, the Storm Cellar can only be destroyed with a Destruction Staff. This option makes the Storm Cellar Giant and Meteor proof.
Note: For those who think this is unbalanced
9 Chest with 81 slots = 108 logs
1 Storm Cellar with 80 slots = 80 logs ,60 rocks ,4 twigs and 1 gold nugget
So the verdict is in, for convenience you must pay more

http://steamcommunity.com/sharedfiles/filedetails/?id=463952377
Controller support! To use, you have to open the inventory using right trigger. See description below for button assignment.

This combines Display Food Values
http://steamcommunity.com/sharedfiles/filedetails/?id=347079953
and Detailed Tooltips
http://steamcommunity.com/sharedfiles/filedetails/?id=360722606
into a single mod that plays nicely. If you want to use either mod seperately you can, but if you want them both running at the same time you have to run this mod and only this mod. (You cannot run the mods listed above at the same time). Here are the details for both.
==Display Food Values==
This mod displays what food and healing items have what hunger, health, sanity values, if cooked values and perish remaining time.
It will work for items in inventory, backpack or in containers.
To see perishtime hold down Ctrl. (Dpad Left on controller)
To see cooked item hold down Alt. (Dpad Right on controller)
To see perishtime of the item if cooked hold down Ctrl and Alt. (Dpad Up on controller)
In mods menu you can press â€˜Configure modâ€™ button and choose the language and enable/disable minimal mode.
Minimal mode will work only if youâ€™ll replace the fonts:
close the game
open mod folder (all mods are in \Steam\steamapps\common\dont_starve\mods);
copy two zip archives from folder new_fonts to folder \Steam\steamapps\common\Donâ€™t Starve Together Beta\data\fonts with replace
run the game
in mods menu press â€˜Configure modâ€™ button and enable minimal mode.
After each update of the game youâ€™ll need to replace the fonts.
==Detailed Tooltips==
Enhances tooltips to display values for: weapon base damage, tool durability, armor condition, armor protection type,armor insulation, and armor damage reduction.
In the config you can choose to turn off different information. In game, if you hold the alt key (DPad up), all of the information is then displayed.

ç‚¹æˆ‘è·³è½¬steamIJN DD - Hibiki(IJN DD -Hibiki)
åŸæ–‡ï¼š

ã€Œä¸æ­»é³¥ã®åã¯ä¼Šé”ã˜ã‚ƒãªã„ã€‚ã€
IJN Destroyer Hibiki, from Kantai Collection, or Kancolle.
(My mods are not skin compatible, aka they canâ€™t use alternate clothing besides gloves, pants/skirts, and shoes, because of the body proportions being different/taller from the default player proportions. Itâ€™s not something I can fix.)
[Latest version: v1.5.0b]
(Please update to the latest version before giving feedback, thank you!)
[Stats (Classic Mode)]
Health: 200
Hunger: 150
Sanity: 100
[Traits/Perks]
General Winter: High cold resistance from being in the Russian Navy.
Survivorâ€™s Guilt: 10% more sanity loss when alone, gains sanity when near other players.
Phoenixâ€™s Resilience: Starts with 200 health, takes 10% less damage.
[Trustworthy]
As of version 1.3.0, Hibiki now starts with lower stats, but each point of damage you take to your health and sanity contributes to an experience system. She can now level up up to 10 times. Each time you level up, Hibiki will usually say a different line depending on your current level and your base stats are increased by 5 (aside from sanity). If other perks are activated, they will also grow stronger as Hibiki levels up. Once Hibiki reaches level 10, she will transform into Verniy, with extra stats and poweredup versions of her own perks. There are two modes, Easy Mode (which is the default) and Hard Mode. In easy mode, if you die above level 5, Hibikiâ€™s level will be decreased by 1 when she gets revived, and her exp gets reset to 0. In hard mode, dying will reset your level to 0.
[Stats and Perks (Trustworthy Mode)]
Health: 150 >> 200
Hunger: 100 >> 150
Sanity: 100
General Winter: Medium cold resistance >> High cold resistance.
Survivorâ€™s Guilt: 15% more sanity loss when alone >> 5% more sanity loss when alone.
Phoenixâ€™s Resilience: Takes 10% less damage >> Takes 20% less damage.
Verniy: Gets a 25% attack boost and moves 1.1x faster.
If you prefer the old version, Trustworthy can be toggled off in the configurations, and she will play exactly like pre 1.3.0 Hibiki. Each of the perks can also be toggled on and off in the mod configurations.
The second ship of the Akatsukiclass Destroyers. This started out as a fairly simple first mod I made to play Dont Starve Together with some friends (and because of a complete lack of Kancolle mods). I eventually added a few more dialogue and functions.
As of 1.5.0, if you have the Modded Skins API mod installed on your server, Hibiki can use an additional skin.

IJN Destroyer Inazuma, from Kantai Collection, or Kancolle.

[Latest version: v1.2.6]
(Please update to the latest version before giving feedback, thank you!)
[Stats]
Health: 150
Hunger: 150
Sanity: 150
[Traits/Perks]
Serious Side: Enters combat mode when struck by lightning.
Truly an Angel: Gives sanity regen to nearby players.
Reluctant Fighter: While not in combat mode, Inazuma deals 25% less damage, but has a 10% chance to dodge attacks.
[Serious Side]
When struck by lightning, Inazuma loses 50 sanity and transforms into her Plasma mode. In this mode, Inazuma moves faster, gains an extra 10% chance to dodge for a total of 20%, and both deal and receive 1.5x damage. Her sanity regen aura turns into a sanity drain aura, and she periodically loses sanity unless itâ€™s raining. Subsequent lightning strikes decrease her sanity by 20. When her sanity goes above 100, she turns back into normal.
Additionally, if she consumes an eggplant while in this state, she loses 20 sanity and returns to normal. In normal mode, she will lose 10 sanity instead.
Just like Hibiki, all her perks are toggleable in the configurations.

ç‚¹æˆ‘è·³è½¬steamShiro | No Game No Life(Shiro |æ²¡æœ‰æ¸¸æˆæ²¡æœ‰ç”Ÿå‘½)
åŸæ–‡ï¼š

Shiro
[Disclosure] I was commisioned to make this mod, thanks to the person who made this happen!
Lore
Shiro is one of the main characters from the anime: â€œNo Game, No Lifeâ€.
One day, Shiro and her brother Sora were playing videogames, until a mysterious being claiming to be a god transported them into a fantasy world.
There they were faced with many challenges along the way, but nothing was a match for the legendary gamer duo, which eventually allowed them to rule over an entire kingdom.
The new queen of games Shiro suddenly stumbled upon a dark portal, curious to see whatâ€™s beyond it, so she entered it alone.
Now she finds herself trapped in Donâ€™t Starve Together, while for others this grim world is quite unpleasant, for Shiro itâ€™s just another game.
Stats
Health:
120
Hunger:
90
Sanity:
75
Perks
[Level Up!]
You become stronger with each enemy you defeat.
Killing an enemy grants you a permanent boost of +1 to all base stats.
You can only double your starting stats.
[Genius]
Your knowledge has no limits, if youâ€™re in the mood.
You gain a bonus to crafting items, based on your current Sanity.
The more Sanity you have, the more things you remember how to craft.
The less Sanity you have, the more things you forget how to craft.
[Cuteness Overload]
You are so adorable, enemies feel bad for hitting you.
Unfortunately, if they do decide to hit you, you get tired much faster.
You take less damage, if you are unarmed.
You take more damage if you have a weapon equipped.
Every time you take a hit from an enemy, it also drains your Hunger.
[Hidden Perk]
You always carry a hidden plushie of your brother, which grants you a passive bonus:
+10% Hunger Resistance
+10% Sanity Drain Resistance
+3% Cold Resistance
+3% Movement Speed
You can type in /bonesaw to play with your brother (Works only if you have no custom gloves on)
Weakneses
Low starting stats.
Canâ€™t take to many hits at once, or else you will be hungry very fast.
Relies on killing mobs early on to acquire a decent amount of strength.
Doesnâ€™t have her brother around.
Starting Items
Golden Axe
Golden Shovel
Golden Pickaxe
Gears
Changelog
(Last Update: 14.01.2017 Version 1.0.7)
Version 0.8.8 Allowed Shiro to play with her brother.
Version 0.9.0 Made the character model mostly compatible with custom clothes, mostly.
Version 0.9.5 Fixed that fancy hair color effect not changing based on lighting.
Version 1.0.0 Steam Workshop Official Release.
Version 1.0.1 Minor tweaks for better compatibility with other mods.
Version 1.0.2 Removed some placeholder stuff and cleaned up mod files.
Version 1.0.3 Fixed a bug where upgraded stats wonâ€™t update properly.
Version 1.0.4 Applied a solution to force changes to character stats to update more aggressively.
Version 1.0.5 Character perk effects now reapply when you reload the game or go in and out of the Caves.
Version 1.0.6 Fixed the game crashing while preloading character attributes.
Version 1.0.7 Fixed Level Up! perk giving way too many stats.
[BUG?]
Due to the way stuff is coded, there appears to be a sort of a builtin delay on applying character stat changes, so what happens is when you kill an enemy your stat upgrade will not be displayed right away.
I have no idea what is causing this weird interaction, this might be just the way the game works, or itâ€™s just a update delay from other mods that show more info about your stats.
Donâ€™t worry, the upgrade perk does actually work and saves your new stats, but what you need to do is make it so that there is a change in your current stats, so for example:
After you kill some monsters, if you eat something that heals you, or you take any damage your new maximum Health with be updated and displayed correctly, if you get hungrier or lose sanity it will show you your new stats.
Thankfully, this issue is mostly visual only and fixes itself during gameplay.
I highly recommend you to download any mod that gives you more info about your stats (like
Combined Status
, for example) and keep an eye on your maximum stats.
Iâ€™m sorry for the inconvenience this might have caused and thank you for playing with my mods and reporting bugs!
Also, check out my DST Touhou Characters:
http://steamcommunity.com/sharedfiles/filedetails/?id=701414094
Cheers, Good Luck and Have Fun! ;)

This is a CLIENT mod. Can be used on any server!
Inspired by the popular mods Display Food Values & Detailed Tooltips, I bring you Item Info.
What this mod does
It displays itemsâ€™ values when hovering over them (hunger, sanity, health, spoilage, insulation [winter/summer], light remaining time, waterproof %, sanity gain/min, uses left and damage) via little icons and a value.
Additionally, it can display your equipped items on a panel on the right (configurable), so that you always know your spearâ€™s uses, your armorâ€™s hp left, or when your torch is going to run out of fuel.
Configuration Options
The default config is just fine, but if you wanna tweak it, here it is:
Info scale: Sets the tooltipâ€™s info scale.
Time format: Change between hours:minutes:seconds and ingame days.
Perish info: Set if you only want to see spoilage time, stale time and then spoilage time, or both.
Show info hands/body/head: If you want to see your equipped itemsâ€™ info.
Equipped Scale: Set the equipped itemâ€™s scale, if you think theyâ€™re too big or too small.
Show prefab name: If you want to know your itemsâ€™ debug spawn name.
Show background: If you wanna see a huge, interfaceblocking background behind your equipped items.
Margin bottom/right: To position the equipped item info.
How to install
Just subscribe to the mod. Thatâ€™s it. This mod displays info in a different way to all others, so no need to replace fonts nor anything like that.
Notes
Like other mods, this mod calculates values based on the itemâ€™s current percent and the base item max values, so the following values might not be 100% exact: perish time, stale time, fuel time, clothes remaining time, uses left, hambat damage.
Controller is supported as of version 0.2
Current issues
Thereâ€™s a bug related to modcomponentactions, which only happens on modded servers, triggered by the way this mod spawns a base item to check its stats. This should make you crash, if you are able to reproduce it please contact me.
Favorite food isnâ€™t supported yet.
New characters since Wortox arenâ€™t supported yet (foods they wonâ€™t eat, food bonuses, damage bonuses, etc). I might make some internal changes to add support for them & modded ones somedayâ„¢
Latest changes
Fixed crash when hovering over trident. Thanks to Grandpa Scout
Fixed equipped items missing. Thanks to ä¹åç”»
Internal changes to pull itemsâ€™ info
Fixed mod not using iceboxes, salt boxes etc. food preserving multiplier
Added salt boxes, Warlyâ€™s pouch support
If you find a bug, have a suggestion or just like this mod, feel free to leave a comment.
If the mod ever breaks please add me as a friend and nag me every day till I fix it.

ç‚¹æˆ‘è·³è½¬steamKoishi Komeiji

Koishi Komeiji, the youkai of the Subconscious from Touhou Project!
Koishi was originally a satori who could read mind of others, but she was hurt by the fear and hatred towards her species. She tried to destroy her mindreading ability by closing her Third Eye. She lost conscious mind in this process, but got the ability to manipulate subconscious. She could no longer be hated, but neither could she be loved, or even remembered by others. She is now a lovely but dreadful youkai motivated by her nature.
Stats
Normal Mode
Health: 135
Hunger: 125
Sanity: 50
Youkai Mode
Health: 270
Hunger: 150
Sanity: 50
Perks
[Unconscious]
Koishiâ€™s sanity wonâ€™t be affected by monsters or darkness.
[Subconscious]
Koishi has 2 states Id and Superego. She has different status in each state.
Id
Faster walking speed, attacking speed, and starve rate, higher damage , and more vulnerable.
Superego
Slower walking speed and starve rate, normal attacking speed, lower damage, and more damage resistance.
[Body of Youkai]
Koishi will restore 0.5HP/s in Youkai Mode. The buffs in both states will be greater and the debuffs will be smaller.
Mechanisms
Subconscious Mechanism
Koishi gains 0.5san/s in Superego and switches to Id when sanity > 48.
Koishi loses 0.5san/s in Id and switches to Superego when sanity < 2.
Koishiâ€™ll become invisible in Superego.Her enemiesâ€™ll quickly forget about her.
Koishiâ€™s Third Eye can switch the state of Koishi. The Eye has a cooldown of 10 seconds.
Koishiâ€™s sanity wonâ€™t be affected by food.
Pseudoego Mechanism
Koishi has another state: Pseudoego. She has very standard stats in this state. She will switch to Superego when sanity < 5, and to Id when sanity > 45.
Koishi gains 0.2san/s in Superego and switches to Pseudoego when sanity > 15.
Koishi loses 0.2san/s in Id and switches to Pseudoego when sanity < 35.
Koishiâ€™s Third Eye can turn on/off her invisibility. Koishi starves much faster than normal when becoming invisible.
Koishiâ€™s sanity will be affected by food.
Spellcards
Dream Signã€ŒAncestors are Watching Youã€
Use Koishiâ€™s power to make beings around fall asleep and experience nightmares. The nonplayer entities which can sleep will all fall asleep for 15 seconds, and will gradually experience nonreduceable health loss. If PVP is enabled, players will also fall asleep and lose 150 sanity. However, if they wake up halfway, they will not experience incoming health and sanity loss. This spellcard has 15s CD and can be used 3 times.
ã€ŒPhilosophy of a Hated Personã€
Project subconscious fear into Koishiâ€™s enemies and make them vulnerable. This forces the enemies to panic for 15 seconds. Meanwhile, they will experience more damage when attacked. The enemies which wonâ€™t panic will take a larger vulnerability. This spellcard has 15s CD and can be used 2 times.
ã€ŒSubterranean Roseã€
Project Koishiâ€™s inner heart to the reality, creating a brambly rose garden around her. This will do huge amounts of damage to enemies around. Bosses in the range will experience an extra health loss. This spellcard has 120s CD and can be used 1 time.
ã€ŒStinging Mindã€
Koishi summons rose mines around her, but then forgets about them immediately. The mines will become less visible after 3s. Any monster stepping on an mine can activate it, causing an explosion that does 50 (100 in Youkai mode) damage per rose to creatures in the range. Players can also activate mines in PVP mode. This spellcard can be used 2 times.
Responseã€ŒYoukai Polygraphã€
Detect any fluctuation in creaturesâ€™ mind to destinguish them. Spawn several rose bands around Koishi. Every rose will deal 10 damage/s to monster around (20 in Youkai Mode), and heal 2 HP/s for alliances. This spellcard cannot be casted again when working, and can be used 1 time.
Memoryã€ŒDNAâ€™s Flawã€
Carve the power of subconsiousness into Koishiâ€™s actions. Each casting can increase 2% moving speed & damage absorption, and 3% damage bonus.This can be done for 10 times. This spellcard can be used 1 time.
Heart Signã€ŒSelfless Loveã€
Koishi inverts the subconsciousness in her actions. Turning her to Id setting sanity to 50 if in Superego, and to Superego setting sanity to 0 if in Id.
If Koishiâ€™s in Pseudoego, she will switch to Id when san > 25. Otherwise she will switch to Superego. This spellcard can be used 4 times.
Instinctã€ŒFreudianã€
Koishi releases the power of subconsciousness state, upgrading her ability for 30 seconds.
Id
Release an impact wave, harm enemies around and push them back, and stun them for 4 seconds. Koishiâ€™s damage bonus and attacking speedâ€™ll increase, but suffers extra damage.
When it ends, summon the wave, harming enemies around and pulling them to Koishi.
Superego
Summon an attraction wave, harm enemies around and pull them towards Koishi, and force them to attack Koishi. Koishiâ€™ll become invincible, but her damage bonus and attacking speed will decrease.
When it ends, release the wave, harming enemies around and pushing them back.
Pseudoego
Summon a shock wave, harm enemies around. Koishiâ€™ll have higher damage bonus, attacking speed and damage absorption.
When it ends, summon a shock wave, harm enemies around.
Items
Koishiâ€™s Hat
: Koishiâ€™s favourite hat, seemingly made of something really hard. It can provide 30% (60% in Youkai Mode) damage absorption and is quite waterproof and insulating. It has very high duration. You can also use flints and rocks to fix it. Can be upgraded at Ancient Altar.
Koishiâ€™s Knife
: A fruit knife thatâ€™s even bigger than a butcherâ€™s knife. It does 40 (65 in Youkai Mode) damage. Koishi can activate her occultism â€œMaryâ€™s Phoneâ€ by rightclicking the knife when equiped. This will allow her to strike further, and teleport to the targetâ€™s back, doubling the damage. This attack will consume 20 hunger (10 in Youkai Mode). Can be upgraded at Ancient Altar.
Koishiâ€™s Third Eye
: Koishiâ€™s noumenon, but somehow becomes detachable after coming to this world. When Koishiâ€™s attacked while equiping it, the tentacles will strike back immediately, dealing 40 (80 in Youkai Mode) damage to the attacker, and it can be used by rightclicking. Its use in each mechanism is listed above. Can be upgraded at Ancient Altar.
Blue Rose
: A beautiful but delicate flower that shouldnâ€™t exist in this world.
When Koishi kills any nonmachine entity, it has a small chance to flourish the soil and grow a blue rose nearby. When Koishi kills an epic enemy, its blood will grow 3 blue roses. She will also spawn blue roses periodically when itâ€™s fullmoon.
It can be picked, but any picker except Koishi will lose health and sanity. The flower can be eaten to restore 2 health and 2 hunger. It can also be used as ingredients for spellcards of Koishi.
Decorative Roses
: These can be decorate your home. They also emit light like fireflies. Decorative roses have different colours and can be crafted by Koishi using a blue rose and a firefly.

Configuration:
Language: switch between English and Chinese
Mode: switch between Normal Mode and Youkai Mode. Koishiâ€™s status will become imba in Youkai Mode
Night vision: switch ON/OFF night vision
Character Mechanism: switch between Subconscious and Ego Mechanism.

Scripts: Hansard
Texture: TimeDicine

This spellcard has 15s CD and can be used 3 times.

Project subconscious fear into Koishiâ€™s enemies and make them vulnerable. This forces the enemies to panic for 15 seconds. Meanwhile, they will experience more damage when attacked. The enemies which wonâ€™t panic will take a larger vulnerability. This spellcard has 15s CD and can be used 2 times.

ã€ŒStinging Mindã€
Koishi summons rose mines around her, but then forgets about them immediately. The mines will become less visible after 3s. Embark on a tropical journey across the seas, Together! Explore a vast new world with new biomes, seasons, and creatures.
Island Adventures brings the seas of
Donâ€™t Starve: Shipwrecked
to Donâ€™t Starve Together.
Key Features
Navigate the Open Ocean:
Craft a boat and set sail together!
Explore an Entirely New World:
Everything is different! Explore new biomes with new resources. Find new sources of food. Survive an array of new creatures out to get you and your friends.
Brave New Seasons:
So long to the old Autumn, Winter, Spring, and Summer. New tropical seasons will try their hardest to kill you all.
Craft New Recipes:
Build new structures and gadgets to help survive the tropics together!

GemCore API
.

here!

to enable various skins for SW items!

ç‚¹æˆ‘è·³è½¬steamSanae Kochiya
åŸæ–‡ï¼š

Sanae Kochiya, the Wind Priestess of Moriya Shrine in Touhou Project, now comes to the DS world!
Sanae is a human, the Wind Priestess of Moriya Shrine, but she is also a distant descendant of the Suwako Moriya, one of the goddesses of Moriya Shrine. She is in charge of gathering faith for the gods, and she also became a minor deity with the power of faith. She has the power of summoning gods of Moriya Shrine and causing miracles to occur. Since the faith competition in Gensokyo is rather drastic, she decides to come to the DS world to tame the residents and gather their faith. Can she survive and successfully gather more faith?
Note: This mod is the beta version, so it might contain bugs. If you find one, please report it as detailed as you can in the comments below, so that I can try to fix the bug!
Stats
Health: 120
Hunger: 90
Sanity: 200
Max Faith: 100
Perks
[Living God]
Sanae is both a human and a god. She can gather faith from others and enhance her power. She has a unique stat of Faith. When there are pigmen, bunnymen and players around, she can collect faith slowly from them. Sanae can also build shrines to collect faith remotely. The higher her current faith is, the higher her walking/attacking speed, damage and resistance, and the slower she starves. The spellcards and skills of Sanae also cost faith. In order to maintain her godship, Sanaeâ€™s faith will degrade naturally at the rate of 0.2/s.
[Youkai Exterminator]
One of the duties of Wind Priestess is youkai extermination. Sanae has witnessed a variety of horrors and is fearless against the monsters in DS world. She will not lose sanity facing monsters, but as a normal girl, sheâ€™s still afaid of the darkness.
Spellcards
Miracleã€ŒNight with Overly Bright Guest Starsã€
Sanae summons a guest star above her head. The guest star will follow Sanae, providing a large range of light and warming the players nearby. The guest star will last for 2 minutes. If itâ€™s raining when casting the spellcard, it will also clear the weather. This spellcard costs 20 faith and can be used twice.
Miracleã€ŒMiracle Fruitã€
Sanae summons 6 miracle fruits around her. It is a veggie type of food, and can restore 5 health, 10 sanity and 8 hunger when eaten. Players who eat the miracle fruit will restore extra 3 health and 5 sanity when eating other veggie of seed fruits within 5 minutes. This spellcard costs 30 faith and can be used once.
Seanceã€ŒFroggy Braves the Wind and Rainã€
Sanae tries to summon the follower frogs of Suwako, but it appears that something goes wrongâ€¦Activates a frog rain that lasts for 30 seconds. This spellcard costs 20 faith and can be used once.
Skills
SkyGod Summon
Press Z key to activate. Sanae summons the power of Kanako Yasaka, the wind god of Moriya Shrine, creating an onbashira that will fall to the position of mouse 2 secods later. When the onbashira lands, all nonplayer entities(PVE mode)/all entities except Sanae(PVP mode) will take 400 physical damage. The onbashira will then disappear slowly. This skill costs 40 faith and has a cooldown of 30 seconds.
EarthGod Summon
Press X key to activate. Sanae summons the power of Suwako Moriya, the mountains god of Moriya Shrine, creating a bubble shield around Sanae. The bubble shield will absorb 400 damage for Sanae, and can persist up to 30 seconds. However, Sanae will still get stunned when attacked. This skill costs 30 faith and has a cooldown of 30 seconds.
Items
Wind Priestessâ€™ Gohei
: The equipment for shrine rituals in Moriya Shrine, blessed by Kanako and Suwako to become exceptionally light and strong. It deals a melee damage of 20, and increases the walkspeed of the holder by 30%. When Sanae is holding the gohei, she can rightclick the gohei to activate Miracleã€ŒGodâ€™s Windã€. When the skill is activated, Sanaeâ€™s attack will become ranged, and each attack will summon a tornado at the target, but each attack also costs 10 faith. When Sanaeâ€™s faith falls beneath 10, the skill will automatically switch off.
Counterfait Suwakoâ€™s Hat
: A mimic product of Suwako Moriyaâ€™s Hat that has a bit of Suwakoâ€™s power on it. It can provide some insulation and waterproofness, and 25% damage reduction. Players which equip the hat can rightclick the hat to hide underground, to avoid being descovered by enemies.
Crystal of Faith
:A crystal of courage and hope, purified from the nightmare. Sanae can consume the crystal and restore 30 faith. So it is that shrine maiden seeketh faiths.
Buildings
Small Branch of Moriya Shrine
A small shrine that is just for visiting activities. This shrine can collect faith from pigmen/bunnymen/players within 20 yards at the rate of 0.2/s, and send the faith to Sanae, wherever she is.
Branch of Moriya Shrine
A proper large shrine for praying and offering activities. This shrine can collect faith from pigmen/bunnymen/players within 30 yards at the rate of 0.4/s, and send the faith to Sanae, wherever she is. Players can offer fuels to the shrine to let it provide lighting. Players can also offer gems, gold, meat and prepared food at the shrine to obtain grace of the godsâ€¦or sometime penalties, depending on what you offered. This function has a cooldown of 30 seconds.
Note: Multiple shrines cannot collect faith more than once from a single prayer, and faith will be offered to the larger shrine in priority. If there are multiple players of Sanae in the map, the faith collected by shrines will be equally devided.
Configuration:
Language: switch between English and Chinese
Max Health/Sanity/Hunger: To set the maximum of Sanaeâ€™s stats
Horizontal/Vertical Position of Faith Bar: To change the position of Sanaeâ€™s faith bar in your interface

Scripts: Hansard
Texture: TimeDicine

Action Queue DST
ported by
xiaoXzzz
has been a great addition to my collection of mods, and it was only after using it for more than a year, that I decided I wanted to undertake fixing the few issues it had.
The original
Action Queue
for Donâ€™t Starve by
simplex
, which was created in 2014, is an amazing mod that still sees much use in its various versions.
Usage
Shift + click on entities as you normally would to add them to the action queue
Shift + doubleclick on an entity to select all entities of the same prefab in a configurable range
Shift + dragclick a rectangle to select entities within a selection box
Shift + dragrightclick with a deployable item in your cursor to place it within the bounded area
Shift + dragrightclick with a tool equipped to focus the actions performed by that tool
Shift + rightclick with a minisign in your cursor to place it directly on a chest
Shift + click on a crafting recipe to continuously craft that item
Press C to craft the last completed recipe (includes structures)
Shift + C to continuously craft the last crafted item (doesnâ€™t include structures)
Press any movement, primary, secondary, attack, or action key to cancel (or pause) the queue
Press F3 to display a turf grid that may help you with aligning your placements
Press F4 to toggle autocollect which is triggered by certain actions
Press F5 to toggle endless deploy mode, ignores selection height to deploy all available items
Config Options
ActionQueue key with an extensive keylist
Always clear queue
(if false, use action key(spacebar) to clear selected targets)
Selection color with 10 colors to choose from
Selection opacity
Double click speed
Double click range
Turf grid toggle key
Turf grid radius
Turf grid color
Option to always deploy on the wall / turf grid
Autocollect toggle key
Enable autocollect by default
Endless deploy toggle key
Enable endless deploy by default
Craft last recipe key
Toothtrap spacing
New Features
Ability to add entities to the selection queue during a deployment action
Autocollect can be toggled in game as needed
Configurable deploy spacing for tooth traps
Caches your last completed recipe to be recalled with a single key press (default C)
Craft last recipe repeatedly with ActionQueue key + last recipe key (shift + C)
Draw added to the action list
Deploy now goes up and down rows instead of always returning to the horizontal start position
Deployment of items by dropping them on the wall grid
Eat added to the action list
Feedplayer added to the action list
Grabs the next stack of items of the same type from your inventory for active item actions
Heal player added to the action list
Minisigns are now easily placeable on chests
Pick action will never target evil flowers
Pickup action will never target any active trap
Pitchfork actions, digging and placing turf
Repeat crafting is faster (timer based)
Tool filtering, which was a feature of the original mod
Unwrap added to the action list
Waits for a broken tool to reequip without canceling the queue
Fixes
ActionQueue should never be canceled by using chat, map, or alttabbing anymore
ActionQueue now cancels properly if you are moving when you release a mouse button during a selection
Fixed incompatibility with Woodie beaver mode
Deployment is only triggered if the selection queue is empty
Give action now works properly with mushroom planters
Selection will not begin if your first click is on a HUD entity
Significantly improved how actions are applied to their targets
Switched to using control handlers for leftclick and rightclick, which means the mod follows rebinds in the games settings menu for primary and secondary keys
Donâ€™t Starve version
ActionQueue Reborn
by
myxal

ç‚¹æˆ‘è·³è½¬steam[Tips]Show attack time for hounds and bosses([æç¤º]æ˜¾ç¤ºçŒçŠ¬å’Œè€æ¿çš„æ”»å‡»æ—¶é—´)
åŸæ–‡ï¼š

function
To prompt the attack time of the hound (worm) and the Boss. The coordinates will be displayed when the Boss already exist. If not, it indicates that the Boss doesnâ€™t fit the conditions for generation.
To display the attack time of the hound and the Bosses of four seasons.
To display the refresh time of the designated creature when instructions are given in the chat window.
The time is in dd:mm:ss format.
instructions
/help tips [to display parameters of tips]
/tips hd [to display the attack time of the hound (worm when in the caves)]
/tips pm [to display the attack time of the pirate]
/tips dr [to display the refresh time of the deer]
/tips dc [to display the attack time of the deerclops]
/tips bg [to display the attack time of the bearger]
/tips ks [to display the refresh time of the Klaus sack]
/tips mt [to display the refresh time of the malbatross]
/tips tt [to display the refresh time of the toadstool]
/tips ck [to display the refresh time of the crabking]
/tips al [to display the time when the antlion gets angry]
/tips df [to display the refresh time of the dragonfly]
/tips ag [to display the cooldown time of the atrium gate]
/tips bh [to display the growth time of the beequeen hive]
/tips lp[to display the cooldown time of the Rift Cycle]
/tips pt [to display the coordinates of the player]
/tips sx x [x is a variable to change the position of UI. If x=0, the UI will be in the center; if x>0, its position will be changed to the right; if x<0, to the left.]
/tips sy y [y is a variable to change the position of UI. If y=0, the UI will be in the center; if y>0, its position will be moved up; if y<0, moved down.]

è¯‘æ–‡ï¼š
ç‚¹æˆ‘è·³è½¬steamBug tracker(é”™è¯¯è·Ÿè¸ªå™¨)
åŸæ–‡ï¼š

More detailed crash logs.
This mod is fully localized, but now I havenâ€™t finished writing the English version of the document, please wait patiently.
What Bug tracker does?
This mod helps you quickly locate the crash point.
[sm.ms]
Log synchronization
When joining a room as a client, if the server has an error, it will only show â€œyou are disconnected from the serverâ€. This mod will send the error message to local.
You can view the log
directly on the client side, whether it is a world with cave or a dedicated server.
Note: Players without administrator privileges cannot view the log and will still only show disconnection screen.
One click to open the log
Click the green text, you can directly get access to the error log.
[sm.ms]
[sm.ms]
Locate bug
Find where bad code is.
Crash point (dark red)
Indicates the actual location where the error occurred. In basic game or in a specific mod.
Traceback (red)
Mod is in the chain that causes errors.
Warning (Yellow)
Mod is not the cause of crash, but it has some other problems of its own.
Safety (green)
No problem.
This feature uses Lua debug trace to analyze mods that cause crashes. The analysis results are for reference only. In the case of a large number of mods, the process of causing a crash can be quite complex, and 100% positioning accuracy is not guaranteed.
Log sending
Found a mod that really has a problem, but donâ€™t know how to notify the author to fix it?
This mod comes with a log sending feature, which sends error messages to the mod developer with a single click. Of course, mod developers have to make adaptations beforehand.
Does the mod have any bugs of its own?
Iâ€™m not sure. If you feel something wrong with it, please contact me.
Message for mod developers

Currently:
å¤æ˜åœ°ãƒœãƒ¼ãƒ«(Code)
The original Mod has stopped updating in 2021, and there are many issues with the current version. Therefore, I (å¤æ˜åœ°ãƒœãƒ¼ãƒ«) will fix this Mod after obtaining authorization. We have obtained authorization from the original author (as requested by B websiteâ€™s private message). Please do not reprint this mod without permission (especially do not transfer to WeGame!!!).
Original mod link:
https://steamcommunity.com/sharedfiles/filedetails/?id=2467616139
Komeiji Satori, the owner of the Underground Hall
Palace of the Earth Spirits in the Touhou Project!
be careful:
If this mod is enabled after generating the world, it can easily cause various problems. It is recommended to enable this mod before generating the world (suspected to be a legacy issue from the original version).
The spellcards cannot be used in the backpack(beside chests,chester and others), it can only be used in the item list.
Main repairs:
Fixed the issue of being able to read but not producing results.
(Possibly) fixed the issue of being actively attacked by spiders.
Fixed various bugs that could not be closed due to overload (if a bug occurred, you can also equip the third eye again to close the overload).
Fixed a bug where the Brain Fingerprint Lie Detection Method crashes when it hits relic furniture, but also removed its ability to block attacks (mainly without removing it, I donâ€™t know why).
Fixed an issue when Satori uses Mental Shock,her sanity raise will stop.
Fixed the issue of Terrible Memories being applied to targets without combo, which could cause the game to crash when the target is attacked.
Fixed the crash when Satori kills a Beasts Trap in UM.
Main changes:
Added weapon: Da Capo, made with complete ancient technology using 40 Nightmare Fuels, infinite durability, attack range is 1.5, restores sanity during attack, and deals a total of 60 damage to the target for 5 segments and 12 points (3rd and 5th segments do not consume player damage multiplier); Right click on the weapon to use a special attack. The distance of the next attack will be changed to 3, and it will consume 10 hunger points. It will deal a total of 150 damage to the target in 3 sections of 50 points. The first and third sections of damage will not consume the playerâ€™s damage multiplier. (At present, it is a glass cutter map when holding it in the hand, and it is also a glass cutter map when throwing it on the ground; it seems that I can hardly change it [Great Mercy].)
CameraShy Rose, will also increase her teammatesâ€™ movement speed.
The panic and blocking attack effects of Mental Shock have been changed to a 20 second immobilization effect in monster mode.
The blocking attack effect of Brain Fingerprint Lie Detection has been changed to a 2.5 second immobilization effect per sustained damage on the damaged unit (in monster mode, 3.5 seconds).
When feeling overloaded, it will maintain a constant temperature of 18 degrees; Correspondingly, the cost of attack and evasion has been increased, and the movement speed is faster when feeling overloaded (1.5x in normal mode), but the speed of hunger consumption (1.2x) and mental consumption (5/min in normal mode, 0/min in monster mode) is also faster.
When equipping the third eye, provide additional basic damage reduction equal to the armor value of the equipment for the sense of consciousness; And an additional 15% increase in perception (25% increase in third eye) and movement speed (not effective when equipped by players outside of perception).
Proposed repairs/changes to the schedule:
Da Capo improves the texture(hard!);
Add Little Oku as a pet (possible);
Add more spellcards.

A coffee port for DST with a twist! Enjoy new coffees and a revised caffeine system (Work In Progress).
The caffeine system is revised in this mod. Instead of just giving you a fixed speed boost for a fixed time after drinking coffee (on/off), this mod gives you a speed boost depending on your
caffeine levels.
Drawbacks of extremely high caffeine levels include gradual sanity and/or health loss with also a tiny chance of fatal overdose!!
Also, this mod adds
Coffee Bushes
and
Coffeebeans
to the world:
â—The default behavior is to generate coffee bushes in hot biomes such as deserts
â—Alternatively there is an option to spawn the â€œCoffee Islandâ€ amongst the vast sea!
For all the people who have already existing worlds
,It is possible to craft Coffee Bushes with a mod setting
The recipe is still experimental.
Please check settings of the mod to toggle on/off whatever mechanic you donâ€™t like, almost everything is optional. :)

ç‚¹æˆ‘è·³è½¬steamDonâ€™t Starve: Dehydrated(ä¸è¦æŒ¨é¥¿ï¼šè„±æ°´)
åŸæ–‡ï¼š

PLEASE NOTICE
Please DO NOT REUPLOAD this mod WITHOUT PERMISSION, regardless of whether they are modified or not. For any modification such as translation, tweak, and/or rebalancing, you must make an addon with dependency for this mod. We will not tolerate any reuploads from now on.
This mod adds a new threat element called â€œthirstâ€ and introduces 32 different beverages and furniture items.
To survive, you now need to consume fluids for hydration.
You can chop down trees to make buckets and obtain water from ponds or lakes, which you might hesitate to drink directly.
For disinfection, you can collect dirty water in suitable containers and boil it over a fire (note: seawater is not suitable).
You can also desalinate seawater to obtain clean water and salt, or dig a well to access groundwater.
There are also wooden barrels available for storing water, which can be useful for preparing for frozen winters when ponds freeze over.
If you find it unsatisfying to only drink water, letâ€™s make a kettle to brew tea. Wally starts with a portable teapot.
If the weather gets hotter and youâ€™re concerned about the spoilage of beverages, letâ€™s try making alcohol with a fermentation vessel. However, always be cautious about excessive drinking.
Letâ€™s explore and try farming for more abundant and effective beverages.
In the forest, you can find tea leaves, and on the moon island, thereâ€™s a coffee bush that holds another secret of the universeâ€¦
Be sure to visit the archive. With the special ingredients you can learn and create there, you might be able to make something incredible in the fermentation vesselâ€¦!
I understand that waiting for endless rain is not an option. Managing a large farm with just a watering can can be challenging.
If you have ingredients with a hint of magic and some technical skills, letâ€™s try making a sprinkler. It might require a lot of effort, but it can make your farming easier and more efficient.
!!TIP!!
Whether itâ€™s an ice cube or a frozen water cup, you can put it in a kettle to boil.
Sprinklers can be installed near freshwater sources that are connected to groundwater. They cannot be installed in hot springs.
Sprinklers are affected by the condition of the connected freshwater source. This means they can freeze or dry up, depending on the situation.
Alcohol gives you the courage to fight proudly from monsters.
